Another disadvantage is that the road and subway are being built downstairs in the hotel, and the noise is very loud every morning. If you really have a light sleeper, you can choose a room near the inside. What I don't understand the most is that the front desk of this hotel has to check the name and phone number for every takeaway order. If it is different from the check-in, the front desk will ask for a long time, and there is no sense of security for personal information. The experience in this area is very poor. There is a **** sister with a bad attitude. The service a**osphere of the whole hotel is very uncomfortable. It can be regarded as the worst room in the Atour I stayed in recently.
